<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Overall, the Marriott was okay with me! We recently stayed at this hotel and had a good experience overall. The hotel is in a great location on the edge of the French Quarter and it's easy to get to everything. Check-in was smooth and easy; the front desk staff was friendly and helpful.After reading many reviews of this hotel, we asked for a room with a view that was on a higher floor. We were placed in the River tower in a corner room with an excellent view. The room was on the smaller size (especially the bathroom which had an oddly low ceiling), however, this is the FQ and space is at a premium. There were three of us in staying in the room and the space was adequate, just a bit smaller than I would like. At first glance, the room is clean but after staying there for a few days, I did notice some areas that needed improvement. The bathtub had been refinished (painted over) and had many scratches. It was also showing signs of slight mildewing. The paint on the doors and trim was dirty and could use some touching up. The blankets and sheets, although clean, could use some replacing due to wear. We also found a pair of shoes under one of the beds (not ours - icky!). On the last night, we decided to get some ice. When we opened the ice bucket, there was a fair amount of water in it even though we hadn't used it during the week we stayed in the room. The bed was very comfortable, we were able to sleep soundly.I did have mixed results with customer service. The first night we checked in there was a problem with the bathtub draining. I called for service and they came quickly and fixed the problem. The same night there was an issue with one of the beds, the comforter smelled, well, not so fresh. I asked if it could be replaced or if they could send up 2 blankets. It took a while, and only 1 blanket was sent up. I called again to ask for another blanket and this time they sent up 2 pillows. I gave up for the night and turned the air conditioning down. The next day I left a note for the maid service and they replaced the comforter. Our last experience with the customer service line happened on our third night. At 2:30 am, a delivery person for room service began knocking on our door (despite the privacy sign on the door). I called customer service to make sure this was not billed to us and to make sure this wouldn't happen again. The woman on the phone (Ethel) said ok and hung up on me! I couldn't believe it so I called back. She said the reason she hung up was that she was surprised as well that this happened. She didn't offer even a simply apology that the hotel had made a mistake.We spoke to the concierge a couple of times and found the woman to be friendly, but not that familiar with the area. She wasn't able to help with anything she didn't have a brochure for (even simple requests on where something was located in the FQ).We drove on this trip and used the valet parking service. It was very convenient and the staff was friendly and helpful (they could help with directions and locations of FQ sites). Please note that parking is expensive, around $23 a night, but it's expensive everywhere in the Quarter.This is a fantastic hotel if you get a great rate through on-line bidding or a good sale. I'm not sure if I would want to pay full price for it. However, we did have a good stay overall and I would stay there again in the future.

<Author>mjdallas
<Content>Loved the New Orleans Marriott The staff was very nice and accomodating. When we checked in we were in a room on the city side and my husband called down to see if we could get moved to a room on the river side. Because several large conventions were in town the Marriott was quite full and the only room they had available was a Studio Suite with a Murphy Bed. We were given that as a choice and we took it. The bed did not have the updated duvet set that the other room had, but the staff changed the bed linen out so that we could have the comforters instead of the old style bedspread. The room had a sitting area, a wet bar with a refrigerator, and our view was spectacular and this more than compensated for having a Murphy Bed. Because my husband is a Platinum Rewards member we have Concierge Lounge privileges. The only pain was that we were not in the same tower as the Lounge so we had to go to the other tower to get to the Lounge. Since we consider the Lounge a bonus and it is open 7 days a week rather than the typical Mon-Fri, we really can't complain about the walk. If I have one complaint, it was the attitude of the the staff in the Concierge Lounge. Instead of being friendly and welcoming like the staff in the other parts of the hotel, it was as if being there was a pain. They were not friendly at all. Since the people using the Lounge are Marriott's Platinum members as well as those people who are paying extra to be on the Concierge Level, I feel that the staff there could have been more welcoming. Also, they did not keep the trays filled and ran out of hor'd'eurves before the end of the time for them (they are supposed to serve from 5:00 - 7:30 and they would run out by 6:00 or 6:30) and the desserts ran out way before the end of the time for them (they are supposed to serve dessert from 8-10 and they would run out by 9 or 9:30). One night it was pouring down rain so we decided to eat at the Riverside Restaurant up at the top of the Marriott. The food was extremely good. When we are in New Orleans we like to eat at the local restaurants and not the hotel restaurants, but this restaurant is quite nice and also has a wonderful view of the city. I would definitely eat there again.  
<Date>Jul 2, 2004

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Could have been cleaner We stayed at the New Orleans Marriot over Memorial Day Weekend and had a great time. The location is excellent and the hotel is beautiful. Our room was small but nicely appointed. The bed was the most comfortable hotel bed I have ever slept in. The pool was indeed cold, even after a day of walking around in the sweltering Louisiana sun. My only complaint was that the room could have been cleaner. The tub had a ring and the sink had some sort of black gunk around the edges. Maid service was not very quick either. We left our room at 10:00 a.m. one morning and the maids had still not been by upon our return at 3:30 p.m. The front door staff was very helpful, assisting me more than once with my stroller, carseat, and ten-month-old. All in all, I would stay at the New Orleans Marriot again.

So close to the river front, the casino (where we enjoyed their excellent breakfast buffet many mornings) and also Bourbon Street and everything else in the French Quarter. We rented bikes right across from the hotel for a day and had a wonderful time touring on those. Went on a swamp tour which was very informative and fun. The Garden District was interesting too. Went on the trolley all the way on St. Charles, the houses were beautiful.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Would Definitely Stay There Again The room was beautiful and spotless. Housekeeping service was regular with no shortage of clean towels and linens. I was very impressed with the staff - everyone was incredibly friendly, helpful, and professional - from the front desk to the doorman to room service. Needed a late check out, and it was not a problem at all. Had none of the hidden fees you sometimes hear about at New Orleans hotels. I had already reccommended the Marriott to several friends before I'd even checked out. Great location on Canal just 2 blocks from Bourbon St., close to French Quarter and Central Business District - great for business or leisure traveller. They are one of the 4-star hotels affiliated with Priceline, so you can get a great deal as well.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Eat, drink and.........Who's Mary? Well, where do I begin?? Hotel was great. I read some poor reviews on this site and was prepared for my room not being cleaned, but this was not the case.... Eventually it was cleaned and all was good for sleeping. This was my first trip to N'awlins and let me tell you.....To-go cups are the best!!! My sister-in law and I had a great time. We booked on Priceline and got a great deal and was not treated poorly for it at this 5 star hotel. (I have read that some hotels dont treat expedia/priceline peeps very nicely) The Hotel staff was very nice. I would only suggest that you ask for a river view if available. Our room had a lovely view of the top of the buildings in part of the French Quarter.... River would have been nicer. The pool was warm, but we didnt go in it. I just had to check since I read it was ice cold on a previous review. The French quarter is definetly within walking distance....and Bourbon street is CRAZY......but Oh so much fun..... I highly recomend a Hurricaine or three and a few Hand Grenades. NO JELLO SHOTS!!! Gray line has the best tours, but check out La Fayette Cemetary on your own. The Garden district tour is cool, but very long and then very brief in the cemetary. (the main reason we went) All and all, Excellent trip, great (but strange) people and dont forget the food.... Take time to eat at the smaller places...... Food is great there!!

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Great Hotel! We stayed at this hotel the weekend of March 13. The staff was friendly and helpful. The hotel was clean and very conveniently located. It is on Canal about halfway between Bourbon and The River. Our room was very clean and nicely furnished. The online pics are very accurate. We had a view of Canal Street. I would suggest that you get a higher room in the River Tower and request the type of view that you would like - Canal St. or the river. If there are no rooms in the River Tower, then request a room with a Canal St. view in the other tower. The restaurant in the lobby has an excellent brunch. We at there twice! We would definitely stay here again.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>FABULOUS My friends and I went to New Orleans on February 12th (which was just as Mardi Gras was starting). We had reservations at another hotel up until the day before we left. I was worried about the hotel because of a review I had read on this site. I had been checking rates, but since it was also Valentine's Weekend, the hotels were outrageous. I decided I'd go on Priceline and try to get a hotel in the French Quarter. To my surprise, I got the Marriott right on Canal Street. It was absolutely fantastic. Walk right outside the door to the parades, right down the street to the casino, down the other way to Bourbon Street, to the street car, to the Ferry. I could not have been happier with this hotel. The wonderful lobby bar was an excellent place to hang out while waiting on another parade. Got it for a steal on priceline.
